Summary\n\n## Issue\nEmpty filter sidebars were appearing in the Django admin even when there were no related objects or choices, creating a confusing user experience with only a generic \"All\" option showing.\n\n## Root Cause Analysis\nThree filter classes had issues with their `has_output()` methods:\n\n1. **RelatedFieldListFilter** - Had overly strict logic that would hide filters that should show\n   - Old condition: `len(self.lookup_choices) + extra > 1`\n   - This prevented single-choice filters from showing (e.g., one related object)\n\n2. **ChoicesFieldListFilter** -
